---
title: "Company Research"
---

In-depth company intelligence report.

NOTE: This is a asynchronous API, which means it will return a report\_id in the response. You would be required to fetch the [report status](https://docs.wokelo.ai/supporting-apis-doc#report-status) and then use [download report](https://docs.wokelo.ai/supporting-apis-doc#download-report) endpoint to obtain the results.

## Request reference

**A sample request**

```json
curl --location --globoff 'https://api.wokelo.ai/api/workflow_manager/start/' \
--header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
--header 'Authorization: your token' \
--data '{
    "workflow": "company_primer",
    "permalink": "tesla-motors"
}'
```

Either of the website/ permalink is mandatory. Ensure that you enter the complete URL of the company (Eg: [https://tesla.com](https://tesla.com)) Industry(optional) should specify company’s industry. Autodetected if left empty.

## Examples

**Company Research**: Company Research report for Salesforce

**Sample Request**

```json
curl --location --globoff 'https://api.wokelo.ai/api/workflow_manager/start/' \
--header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
--header 'Authorization: your token' \
--data '{
    "workflow": "company_primer",
    "permalink": "salesforce"
}'
```

                        "title": "Product And Services",
                        "answers": [
                            "**Sales Cloud** fuses human sellers with AI agents for prospecting, performance management and revenue intelligence, while **Service Cloud** automates omni-channel support, routing and field service.",
                            "**Marketing Cloud** and **Commerce Cloud** deliver personalized journeys and unified shopping, all enriched by **Data Cloud**’s hyperscale customer graph and by agentic capabilities that generate content and offers.",
                            "The **Salesforce Platform** offers low-code development, governance via the Trust Layer and global deployment through **Hyperforce**, and is extended by **Agentforce** which lets customers create autonomous AI workforces.",
                            "**Slack**, **MuleSoft Integration**, **Tableau Analytics**, **Starter Suite** for SMBs and vertical clouds like **Industries AI** round out a portfolio designed to connect data, collaboration, automation and insights on one trusted platform."
                        ]
                    },
                    {
                        "title": "Business Model",
                        "answers": [
                            "Revenue is generated primarily from term-based **subscription** contracts, typically **12–36 months**, recognized ratably and supplemented by professional services and premier support.",
                            "A multi-tenant SaaS architecture spreads infrastructure costs, while the **AppExchange** marketplace and API economy create network effects and incremental monetization from ISVs.",
                            "Sales are driven by a global direct sales force augmented by SIs and resellers who receive first-year referral fees, and by consumption-based pricing for newer products like **Data Cloud** and **Agentforce**.",
                            "Free and low-cost trails, no-code tooling and an ecosystem of **tens of millions of Trailblazers** lower customer acquisition cost and seed future upsell opportunities across the portfolio."
                        ]
                    },

                        "answers": [

                            "The go-to-market plan stresses international expansion, investing in local **Hyperforce** infrastructure and partner marketplaces to reach enterprises of all sizes in every major region.",
                            "Product road-maps pivot around verticalized AI, highlighted by the launch of **Agentforce** and **Industries AI**, to position Salesforce as the trusted operating system for autonomous agents.",
                            "A disciplined capital allocation framework favors bolt-on and transformational M&A and strategic minority investments that accelerate roadmap gaps, add industry depth and drive operating leverage."

        "Business Model Overview": {
            "business_model_insights": [
                {
                    "area": "Customer Segments",
                    "details": [
                        "Salesforce serves over 150,000 customers globally across diverse organizational sizes and industries, with enterprise clients averaging 3.3 different clouds per customer, demonstrating platform stickiness and cross-sell success",
                        "Professional Services represents 29.2% of the customer base, leveraging tailored CRM solutions for enhanced service delivery and operational efficiency across accounting, consulting, legal, and staffing firms",
                        "Manufacturing comprises 11% of customers, using specialized solutions like Manufacturing Cloud for supply chain optimization, demand forecasting, and partner relationship management",
                        "Financial Services accounts for 9% of users, including banks, insurance companies, and wealth management firms utilizing Financial Services Cloud for regulatory compliance and client lifecycle management",
                        "Retail encompasses 7.8% of customers, deploying commerce solutions for digital sales automation, personalized customer engagement, and omnichannel experiences across fashion, grocery, and mass merchant sectors"
                    ]
                },
                {
                    "area": "Value Proposition",
                    "details": [
                        "The core differentiator is Salesforce's deeply unified \"one piece of code\" platform architecture that integrates Customer 360 applications, Data Cloud, and Agentforce AI on a single codebase, eliminating system complexity and ensuring seamless data flow",
                        "Agentforce platform represents a multibillion-dollar AI product line providing autonomous agents that handle 40% of work across sectors, delivering significant productivity enhancements and operational intelligence at scale",
                        "Comprehensive AI integration through Einstein platform embeds predictive and generative AI across all clouds, with the Einstein Trust Layer ensuring secure, compliant, audit-ready AI deployments as a vital technical differentiator",
                        "Industry-specific clouds for healthcare, financial services, government, and manufacturing provide regulatory compliance and specialized workflows, strengthening adoption in regulated sectors"
                    ]
                },
                {
                    "area": "Revenue Model",
                    "details": [
                        "Subscription and Support Services generate over 93% of revenue with FY 2025 totaling approximately $37.9 billion, including Sales Cloud ($8.32 billion), Service Cloud ($9.05 billion), and Platform and Other ($7.25 billion)",
                        "Hybrid pricing model combines per-user subscriptions with consumption-based pricing for AI products like Agentforce and Data Cloud, generating $1.2 billion in annual recurring revenue with 120% year-over-year growth",
                        "Sophisticated tiered pricing structure ranges from Starter Suite ($25 per user/month) to specialized solutions like Agentforce 1 Sales ($550 per user/month), enabling market penetration across SMBs to enterprises",
                        "Professional Services comprise 6% of revenue ($2.22 billion in FY 2025), essential for driving adoption and supporting client-specific digital transformation projects"
                    ]
                },
                {
                    "area": "Go-to-Market Strategy",
                    "details": [
                        "Cloud-first, subscription-based delivery model with rapid deployment capabilities serves both SMEs and large enterprises, supported by the AppExchange marketplace offering access to over 200 partners and pre-built solutions",
                        "Robust partner ecosystem encompasses ISVs, resellers, and consultants like Accenture and Deloitte enabling channel sales and custom implementations, with strategic alliances including AWS and Google Cloud for multicloud environments",
                        "Global market expansion prioritizes untapped regions with $1 billion investment in Singapore, while nearly half of top 100 recent wins are international, demonstrating global reach and adaptability",
                        "Scaling sales capacity and accelerating adoption of Agentforce and Data Cloud are top execution priorities, supported by over 12,000 customers including Dell, FedEx, and PepsiCo"
                    ]
                },

                    "area": "Technology & IP",
                    "details": [

                        "Data Cloud and integrations with Informatica and MuleSoft's Anypoint Platform enable robust workflow orchestration and data harmonization, achieving considerable adoption and growth",
                        "High customer stickiness reflected in #1 market share (23%+) with over 150,000 customers including Fortune 500 companies, emphasizing platform lock-in effects and exceptional retention rates"

                    "summary": "**AI Integration and Innovation**\n\n**Salesforce** integrates sophisticated artificial intelligence technologies throughout its cloud CRM platform, such as **Sales AI**, **Marketing AI**, **Customer Service AI**, **Commerce AI**, and the **Einstein Platform**. These tools automate critical CRM functions, deliver predictive insights, and personalize customer engagement in real-time. Productivity enhancements extend to platforms like **Slack** via AI-powered workflows, leading to efficient collaboration and immediate access to key data. The use of agentic AI—autonomous systems capable of reasoning, planning, and executing tasks—further differentiates **Salesforce** by enabling advanced workflow automation and multistep processes with minimal human input, directly optimizing customer outcomes and business efficiency. [1-6]\n\nThrough strategic acquisitions and the integration of companies like **Informatica**, **Salesforce**'s AI agents benefit from best-in-class data management and governance, ensuring clean, reliable enterprise data for decision-making and mitigating risks like \"AI hallucinations.\" This trust in AI-derived insights places **Salesforce** at the forefront of intelligent CRM solutions. [5]\n\n**AI-driven personalization** has directly contributed to measurable industry outcomes, such as a 30% increase in digital revenue at **Heathrow Airport** with **Salesforce**'s automated service tools, highlighting the practical impact and competitive edge of its AI capabilities. [4]\n\n**Platform Architecture and Unified Ecosystem**\n\n**Salesforce**'s CRM is constructed on a robust, scalable, and unified platform architecture—such as **Hyperforce** and **Agentforce 360**—supporting deep customization and seamless integration for organizations of all sizes, from startups to global enterprises. Specialized environments like **Government Cloud Plus** and **MuleSoft Government Cloud** provide secure, regulation-compliant operations, broadening the solution’s industry reach. [1-6]\n\nThe unified approach means that all critical business functions—sales, service, marketing, IT—are managed via a single integrated system, improving operational agility and cost-effectiveness. The architecture’s flexibility supports business growth, allowing companies to scale and only pay for what they use. [3,6]\n\n**AppExchange** and **AgentExchange** represent unique marketplace ecosystems within **Salesforce**. They enable customers to deploy pre-built or custom AI solutions rapidly, integrate seamlessly with third-party applications, and tap into a vast partner network for creative solution extensions. These features dramatically expand organizational capability without significant development effort, further distinguishing **Salesforce** from its competitors. [1,4,6]\n\nIntegration with platforms such as **Data 360** and **MuleSoft**—enhanced by **Informatica’s** data governance—supports a single, unified “source of truth” for enterprise data. This eliminates silos, improves data-driven decision-making, and supports compliance and ethical AI standards across industries. [5]\n\n**Industry Impact and Market Leadership**\n\n**Salesforce** is consistently recognized as the leading global cloud CRM provider, holding a dominant market share (23.8%) over competitors such as **SAP**, **Microsoft**, and **Oracle**, which each hold about 5% individually. This leadership is reinforced by continuous product innovation, high-profile strategic acquisitions (e.g., **Tableau**, **Slack**), and a strong focus on R&D. [7]\n\nThe platform has broad adoption—serving over 150,000 companies including major enterprises such as **Amazon Web Services** and **Toyota**—and offers tailored, vertical-specific CRM applications for unique industry demands. The scale and depth of **Salesforce**'s ecosystem magnify its industry-wide impact. [7]\n\nBy driving multi-cloud and cross-departmental integration, **Salesforce** enables organizations to unify customer and operational records, enhancing customer experiences and reporting accuracy. Its data harmonization and intelligence-driven solutions are cited as key factors in transforming the digital enterprise landscape. [5]\n\n**Competitive Positioning and Analyst Perspectives**\n\n**Salesforce** distinguishes itself through a deeply unified platform that combines apps, data, and autonomous AI agents in a “one piece of code” system. This Trinity is highlighted by company leadership as being “light years ahead” of other providers, eliminating the need for customers to self-assemble disparate solutions and thereby enhancing productivity, efficiency, and user experience at scale. [8]\n\nThe company’s autonomous AI—epitomized by **Agentforce**—provides an “agent-first” architecture, contrasting with rivals like **Microsoft Copilot**, which **Salesforce** claims to be only a repackage of **ChatGPT** with less integration and flexibility. **Salesforce**'s competitive advantage is further cemented by its high customer success and satisfaction rates, robust switching costs, and a vast, highly interconnected data ecosystem that intensifies customer lock-in. [9-10]\n\nKey industry analysts and financial commentators highlight **Salesforce**’s commitment to continuous R&D, a strong vision for leading the “digital labor revolution,” and investments in agentic AI as central to its sustained differentiation and market leadership. [11-12]\n\nThe company maintains its number one **CRM** ranking by **IDC Software Tracker** for 11 consecutive years, underscoring its unparalleled status in the market and effectiveness of its unified, AI-driven technology strategy. [13]\n\n**Financial Outcomes and Industry Leadership**\n\nRobust investment in technology and innovation correlates directly with financial performance: **Salesforce**'s revenue rose from $21.25 billion in 2021 to $37.89 billion in 2025, alongside further improvements in EBITDA and net income margins. These financial gains spotlight the success of technology-driven growth strategies and reinforce **Salesforce**'s leadership in the CRM sector. [14]\n\nContinuous R&D spend—exceeding $10 billion since **FY ‘24**—drives the evolution of **Salesforce**'s cloud and AI offerings, ensuring sustained technological leadership and adaptation to new enterprise needs. [12]"

This platform consolidates data, applications, and AI-driven automation, ensuring all customer-facing departments have access to a single, real-time view of each customer. The seamless integration supports end-to-end customer lifecycle management, fostering enhanced engagement by avoiding fragmented workflows and redundant processes [1-5]\n\nIntegration of solutions like **Sales Cloud**, **Service Cloud**, and **Marketing Cloud** allows these business functions to operate through a single codebase, streamlining customer data sharing and interactions. These AI-driven capabilities allow for targeted customer engagement at every touchpoint, from automated lead management to tailored marketing messages and proactive customer support resolutions [1-6]\n\nThe automation of complex workflows—such as lead qualification, case assignment, and marketing campaign execution—helps reduce manual errors, ensure prompt customer responses, and enable service representatives to focus on high-value interactions, further fostering customer engagement and satisfaction [1-6]\n\n**Degree Customer Insights and Cross-Functional Collaboration**\n\nWith unified data access via tools like **Data Cloud** and **Customer 360 Audiences**, **Salesforce** provides a comprehensive view of each customer, consolidating interactions and behavioral data from all departments.
